[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

-------------------

[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I structured this JSON-formatted Questionnaire for you:
```
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WEPLACEENV",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _TF_QUESTIONS:[
              {"code1","How would rate your overall satisfaction with the workplace environment?"},
               ["Very Satisfied", 5],
                [Slightly satisfied,4]
                 ['Not very satisfying',2],['Extremely dissatisfying' ,0]]
             ]
           }
         ]

```
This questionnaire is designed to assess employees’ perceptions of their work place.

 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

Explanation:

Here's how I structured this JSON-formatted questionnaire for you.

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"EWR001",
          "NAME":"",
           "TYPE_ID" :3,
            "_TF_QUESTIONS":[ 
              {  
                CODE: 'Q1',
                 NAME:'What was the reason for ending this working relationship?',
                  TYPE_ID': 2,   
                   DISPLAY_ORDER' :0 ,    
                    '_TF_ANSWERS':
                      [
                        {"ANSWER": "Mutual agreement"},
                          {"ANSWER":"Change in job requirements"}, 
                            {   ANSWEAR: 'Layoff or downsizing'},  
                              {'ANsweaR':  Other (please specify) }
                       ]
              },
               {
                CODE:'Q2',
                 NAME:"How would you rate the communication during this working relationship?",
                  TYPE_ID' :3,   
                   DISPLAY_ORDER ':1 ,    
                    '_TF_ANSWERS':
                      [
                        {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},
                          {   ANSWEAR: 'Good'}, 
                            {'ANsweaR':  Fair},  
                              {'ASnswEAr':'Poor'}
                       ]
              },
               {
                CODE:'Q3',
                 NAME:"What was the most significant challenge you faced during this working relationship?",
                  TYPE_ID' :1,   
                   DISPLAY_ORDER ':2 ,    
                    '_TF_ANSWERS':
                      [
                        {"ANSWER": "Lack of resources"},
                          {   ANSWEAR: 'Difficulty in meeting deadlines'}, 
                            {'ANsweaR':  Other (please specify) }
                       ]
              },
               {
                CODE:'Q4',
                 NAME:"How would you rate the overall performance during this working relationship?",
                  TYPE_ID' :3,

                      [

                          {   ANSWEAR: 'Good'}, 
                            {'ANsweaR':  Fair},

                       ]
              }
            ]

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based Questionnaire for you:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"EMPLOYEE_FEEDBACK",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _tf_questions":[]
         }
       ]
   }

```

Here's the questionnaire content step by step:

1. Introduction:
```json
{
  CODE:"INTRO_EMPFEEDBKQSTN", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :0,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: "Welcome to our Employee Feedback Questionnaire! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve the work environment and employee experience. Please answer these questions honestly."
               }
             ]
}
```

2. Overall Satisfaction:
```json
{
  CODE:"OVERALL_SATISFACTION", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :1,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: "How satisfied are you with your overall job experience?"
                 },
               {ANSWER: "Very Satisfied"},
                  {"Not Very Satisified"}
             ]
}
```

3. Job Responsibilities:
```json
{
  CODE:"JOB_RESPONSIBILITIES", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :2,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: ""
                 },
               {ANSWER: "I have the right amount of work to do."},
                  {"Too little"},
                    {"To much"}
             ]
}
```

4. Communication:
```json
{
  CODE:"COMMUNICATION", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :3,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: "How would you rate the communication within your team?"
                 },
               {ANSWER: ""},
                  {"Not Very Good"}
             ]
}
```

5. Feedback:
```json
{
  CODE:"FEEDBACK", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :4,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: "What do you think we could improve on to make your job more enjoyable?"
                 },
               {ANSWER: ""},
                  {"Not Sure"}
             ]
}
```

6. Suggestions:
```json
{
  CODE:"SUGGESTIONS", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :5,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: "Do you have any suggestions for improving the work environment?"
                 },
               {ANSWER: ""},
                  {"Not Sure"}
             ]
}
```

7. Closing:
```json
{
  CODE:"CLOSING", 
    NAME:"",
      DISPLAY_ORDER :6,  
        "_TF_ANSWERS":
          [
              {
                ANSWER: "Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our workplace."
                 },
               {ANSWER: ""},
                  {"Not Sure"}
             ]
}
```

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based Questionnaire:

1. The root of my questionnaire contains a single property 'data'.
2. This data object has one and only 7 questions.
3 Each question is represented by an array element in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' field, which itself resides within another level called "CODE" for each individual's unique code.

        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.

The admitted question's types are the following:

 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Learner feedback after a course session

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here's how I structured this JSON:

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"LearnerFeedback",
          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID" :3,
        	"_TF_QUESIONS":[],
       }
     ]
}
```

Here's the questionnaire content step by step:

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTNAIRES":
      [
        {
            "CODE":"LearnerFeedback",
           "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID" :3,
        	"_TF_QUESIONS":[ 
              {  
                CODE: 'Q1',
               NAME:'How would you rate the overall quality of this course session?',
                 TYPE_ID': 2, // Multiple Choice
                  DISPLAY_ORDER' :'0',   
                   '_Tf_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {
                        ANSWER : "Excellent"
                       },
                     { 
                         ANSWER: 'Good'
                          },  
                           {'ANSWER':'Fair'}
                            ,{'ANSWer':"Poor"}
                             ]
               } ,
              // Q2 - Rating
            	{   
                CODE:'Q3',
                 NAME:"How would you rate the instructor's presentation style?",
                  TYPE_ID': 1, 
                   DISPLAY_ORDER' :'0',  
                    '_Tf_ANSWERS':
                     [
                       { ANSWER: "Excellent" },
                      {'ANSWER':"Good"},
                        {"Answer":"Fair"}
                          ,{"AnsWer": 'Poor'}
                           ]
               } ,
              // Q3 - Multiple Choice
            	{   
                CODE:'Q4',
                 NAME:"What did you find most valuable about this course session?",
                  TYPE_ID': 2, 
                   DISPLAY_ORDER' :'0',  
                    '_Tf_ANSWERS':
                     [
                       { ANSWER: "The instructor's expertise" },
                      {'ANSWER':"Hands-on practice"},
                        {"Answer":"Networking opportunities"}
                          ,{"AnsWer": 'Other'}
                           ]
               } ,
              // Q4 - Rating
            	{   
                CODE:'Q5',
                 NAME:"How likely are you to recommend this course session?",
                  TYPE_ID': 3, 
                   DISPLAY_ORDER' :'0',  
                    '_Tf_ANSWERS':
                     [
                       { ANSWER: "Very Likely" },
                      {'ANSWER':"Somewhat Likley"},
                        {"Answer":"Not Very Likey"}
                          ,{"AnsWer": 'Not at All'}
                           ]
               } ,
              // Q5 - Open-ended
            	{   
                CODE:'Q6',
                 NAME:"What suggestions do you have for improving future course sessions?",
                  TYPE_ID': 4, 
                   DISPLAY_ORDER' :'0',  
                    '_Tf_ANSWERS':
                     [
                       { ANSWER: "" }// Text field to collect open-ended feedback
                        ]
               }
            ]   
          },
        "NAME":"Learner Feedback",
       "_TF_QUESTIONS":
         []
      ],
    }]
}
```

This questionnaire includes 6 questions:

1. How would you rate the overall quality of this course session? (Multiple Choice)
2-3: Rating and Multiple choice to assess instructor's presentation style
4,5 : Likelihood scale for recommending future sessions 
And an open-ended question that allows learners provide their suggestions

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500000005
     - Topic: Course feedback
     - Question number: 5
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Course feedback

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based Questionnaire for "Course Feedback":

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"CF001",
          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
        	"_TF_QUESTIONS":[

            // Section: Overall Course Satisfaction 
             {
              "CODE":"Q1",  
               "NAME":"'How satisfied are you with this course?' ",   
                "_TF_ANSWERS":
                  [
                    {"ANSWER","Very Satisfied"},
                     {{"Slightly Unsatisfactory"}},
                      {{"Not Very Dissatisified"}}
                   ]
            },
            
             // Section: Course Content
              {
                 CODE":"Q2",  
               "NAME":"'How relevant is the course material to your goals?' ",   
                "_TF_ANSWERS":
                  [
                    {"ANSWER","Very Relevant"},
                     {{"Somewhat Relevent"}},
                      {{"Not Very Relavant"}}
                   ]
            },
            
             // Section: Instructor Performance
              {
                 CODE":"Q3",  
               "NAME":"'How effective is the instructor in teaching this course?' ",   
                "_TF_ANSWERS":
                  [
                    {"ANSWER","Very Effective"},
                     {{"Somewhat Affective"}},
                      {{"Not Very Effectve"}}
                   ]
            },
            
             // Section: Learning Experience
              {
                 CODE":"Q4",  
               "NAME":"'How engaging is the course learning experience?' ",   
                "_TF_ANSWERS":
                  [
                    {"ANSWER","Very Engaging"},
                     {{"Somewhat Enagging"}},
                      {{"Not Very Eenging"}}
                   ]
            },
            
             // Section: Course Organization
              {
                 CODE":"Q5",  
               "NAME":"'How well is the course organized?' ",   
                "_TF_ANSWERS":
                  [
                    {"ANSWER","Very Well"},
                     {{"Somewhat Organized"}},
                      {{"Not Very Orgnaizd"}}
                   ]
            },
            
             // Section: Additional Feedback
              {
                 CODE":"Q6",  
               "NAME":"'Any additional feedback or suggestions you have for the course?' ",   
                "_TF_ANSWERS":
                  [
                    {"ANSWER","Open-ended text field"}
                   ]

```

This questionnaire is designed to gather students' opinions on their learning experience in a specific Course. It covers various aspects such as overall satisfaction, relevance of material, instructor performance and more.

Feel free ask me if you want any changes or modifications!

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100004
     - Topic: Access to Technology and Tools
     - Question number: 9
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Access to Technology and Tools

                    ...]
        }

        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"CPCLARITY",
          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
           _TF_QUESTIONS:[
            {"code1","What is your current job title?", TYPE:ID, DISPLAY_ORDER:"0", ANSWERS:["Software Engineer Intern (Current)"]},
             {{"How would you rate the clarity of career goals in our company?" , QUESTION_TYPE : ID}, "DISPLAY ORDER": 2,"ANSWERS":["Very Clear" ,"Somewhat Unclear","Not at All Clearly Defined"]}
            {"What motivates your desire for a clear path forward?", TYPE:ID, DISPLAY_ORDER:"3", ANSWERS:["Sense of accomplishment and fulfillment in my work"]},
             {{"How often do you feel uncertain about the next steps to achieve career growth?" , QUESTION_TYPE : ID}, "DISPLAY ORDER": 4,"ANSWERS":["Almost Never" ,"Occasionally","Mostly"]}
            {"What are some specific skills or areas where I'd like more training and development?", TYPE:ID, DISPLAY_ORDER:"5", ANSWERS:["Data Analysis for Business Insights"]},
             {{"How would you rate the support from your manager in achieving career goals?" , QUESTION_TYPE : ID}, "DISPLAY ORDER": 6,"ANSWERS":["Very Supportive" ,"Somewhat Supported","Not at All"]}
            {"What are some potential roadblocks that might hinder my progress towards a clear path forward?", TYPE:ID, DISPLAY_ORDER:"7", ANSWERS:["Lack of resources or budget"]},
             {{"How would you rate the overall satisfaction with your current career?" , QUESTION_TYPE : ID}, "DISPLAY ORDER": 8,"ANSWERS":["Very Satisfied" ,"Somewhat Unsatisfying","Not at All"]}
            {"What are some potential next steps I could take to achieve a clearer path forward?", TYPE:ID, DISPLAY_ORDER:"9", ANSWERS:["Seek mentorship or coaching"]},
             {{"How would you rate the confidence in your ability to navigate career changes?" , QUESTION_TYPE : ID}, "DISPLAY ORDER": 10,"ANSWERS":["Very Confident" ,"Somewhat Uncertain","Not at All"]}
          ]
        }
      ],
    },
}
```

This questionnaire is designed for employees seeking clarity on their current and future careers.

            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.

 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

Generate me a questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-formatted questionnaire for you:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE" : "FBM001",
          "NAME":"Feedback mechanisms survey ",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
        	"_TF_QUESTIONS":[

            // Question: How often do we receive feedback from our team members?
			{
              "CODE":@"Q1-01", 
			  "NAME":"'How would you rate the frequency of receiving constructive criticism or positive reinforcement?'",
			 TYPE_ID : 2,  
             "_TF_ANSWERS":
               [
                 {"ANSWER":'Never'},
			     {{"Answer":"Rarely"},
			  	{“Answer”:’Sometimes”},
			    {'"Answer': 'Frequently'}
              ]
            },
            
		 // Question: What do you think about the current feedback mechanisms in place?
          {
             "CODE":@"Q1-02", 
			 “NAME":'What are your thoughts on our existing methods for sharing and acting upon constructive criticism or positive reinforcement?'",
		     TYPE_ID : 4,  
	         "_TF_ANSWERS":
	           [
	             {"ANSWER":"They work well"},
			     {“Answer”:’Sometimes they do'},
			    {'"Answer': 'Not very effective'}
              ]
            },
            
		 // Question: How important is it to you that we have a feedback mechanism in place?
          {
             "CODE":@"Q1-03", 
			 “NAME":'How crucial would having an efficient and reliable method for sharing constructive criticism or positive reinforcement be?'",
		     TYPE_ID : 3,  
	         "_TF_ANSWERS":
	           [
	             {"ANSWER":"Very important"},
			     {“Answer”:’Somewhat Important”},
			    {'"Answer': 'Not very significant'}
              ]
            },
            
		 // Question: What would you like to see changed about our current feedback mechanisms?
          {
             "CODE":@"Q1-04", 
			 “NAME":'What changes or improvements do we need in order for the existing methods of sharing constructive criticism and positive reinforcement?'",
		     TYPE_ID : 2,  
	         "_TF_ANSWERS":
	           [
	             {"ANSWER":"More frequent feedback"},
			     {“Answer”:’Clearer expectations'},
			    {'"Answer': 'Anonymous reporting'}
              ]
            }
          ]

        }

      ] 
    } 

}
```
This questionnaire is designed to gauge the effectiveness of current Feedback Mechanisms and gather suggestions for improvement.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100018

     - Question number: 9
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-formatted questionnaire for you:
```
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"FBM001",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _tf_questions":[
              {"code":"","name","What do we currently use to gather feedback from employees?"},
                ["_type_id",1,"DESCRIPTION"],
                  DISPLAY_ORDER":0},
               "_TF_ANSWERS":
                 [
                   {ANSWER:"Email Surveys"}, 
                    ANSWER":"In-Person Meetings"}]}],
```

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

                     {'Answer' :"No"},
                      ]
                 },
              {
                code: '_q3',
               name : 'What motivates you to consider internal mobility opportunities?',
             type_ID   ,4,
            display_Order 1,"_tf_answers": 
                   [ {"answer":"Career growth and development"},{'ANSWER':"New challenges"},{"Answer" :"Better work-life balance"} ]
              },
                {
                  code: '_q5',
                 name : 'What would make you more likely to consider internal mobility opportunities?',
               type_ID   ,1,"display_order ":2,
             "_tf_answers": 
                   [ {"answer":"Clear career path and growth prospects"},{'ANSWER':"More job security"},{"Answer" :"Better compensation"} ]
                },
              {
                 code: '_q7',
                  name : 'How important is internal mobility to you?',
               type_ID   ,3,"display_order ":4,
             "_tf_answers": 
                   [ {"answer":"Very Important","weighting " 5},{"ANSWER";"Somewhat Important", weighting"2"},{"Answer"" Not VeryImportant"} ]
              }
            ]

    }

}
```
This questionnaire is designed to gauge the respondents' interest in internal mobility opportunities, what motivates them and their expectations from such a move.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

      [

          "NAME":"",

```

Here's your Kick-off Meeting Feedback Questionnaire:

```json

{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":[
       { 
         CODE: 'Kickoff_Meeting_Feedback',
          NAME:'What did you think of the kick off meeting?',
           TYPE_ID':3,
            _F_QUESTIONS:[
               // Question about overall satisfaction with kickoff.
              {"CODE": "Overall_Satisfaction",
                "NAME":"How satisfied were  you with this Kick-off Meeting?",
                 'TYPE_ID':'1', 
                  '_TF_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {ANSWER: 'Very Satisfied'},
                     {'Answer': 'Somewhat Satisfaction'},  
                       ...,
                   ]},
               // Question about meeting's content.
              {"CODE": "Content",
                NAME:"What did you think of the topics covered in this Kick-off Meeting?",
                 TYPE_ID:'1', 
                  '_TF_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {ANSWER: 'Very Relevant'},
                     {'Answer':  Somewhat Relevent'},  
                       ...,
                   ]},
               // Question about meeting's organization.
              {"CODE": "Organization",
                NAME:"How well was this Kick-off Meeting organized?",
                 TYPE_ID:'1', 
                  '_TF_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {ANSWER: 'Very Well'},
                     {'Answer':  Somewhat Organized'},  
                       ...,
                   ]},
               // Question about meeting's length.
              {"CODE": "Length",
                NAME:"How long did you think this Kick-off Meeting should have been?",
                 TYPE_ID:'1', 
                  '_TF_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {ANSWER: 'Too Long'},
                     {'Answer':  Just Right'},  
                       ...,
                   ]},
               // Question about meeting's engagement.
              {"CODE": "Engagement",
                NAME:"How engaged were you during this Kick-off Meeting?",
                 TYPE_ID:'1', 
                  '_TF_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {ANSWER: 'Very Engaged'},
                     {'Answer':  Somewhat Disengaging'},  
                       ...,
                   ]},
               // Question about meeting's feedback.
              {"CODE": "Feedback",
                NAME:"What suggestions do you have for improving future Kick-off Meetings?",
                 TYPE_ID:'4', 
                  '_TF_ANSWERS':
                    [
                      {ANSWER: 'More Interactive'},
                     {'Answer':  More Relevant Topics'},  
                       ...,
                   ]},
            ]
         }
       ],
     }   
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather feedback from participants about the kick-off meeting. It includes questions that assess overall satisfaction, content relevance, organization effectiveness and engagement level during the event as well

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100031
     - Topic: Leadership Effectiveness
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Leadership Effectiveness

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-formatted questionnaire for you:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"LEADERSHIP_EFFECTIVENESS",
          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
          "_TF_QUESTIONS":[]
       }
     ]
   }

```

Here's the questionnaire content step by step:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
        	"CODE":"LEADERSHIP_EFFECTIVENESS",
            "NAME":"",
			"type_id:3,
          _tf_questions":[

           // Question1 
             {"code":"Q_01","name":"","typeId":2,"displayOrder":0, "_TF_ANSWERS":
              [
                {answer:"Strongly Agree"},
				{Answer:"Somewhat agree"}
               ]
            },
            
		   
		   {
		     "CODE":"",
		       NAME:"",
		      TYPE_ID:1,
		    DISPLAY_ORDER:;
             _tf_answers:

The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

      [

          "NAME":"",

         _tf_questions":[]
       }
     ]
   }

```

Here's the questionnaire on Pressure at work:

**Work Pressures Questionnaire**

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTNAIRES":
      [
        {
            CODE:"work_pressure",
          NAME:"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
         _tf_questions":[

              // Q1. How often do you feel overwhelmed by your workload?
               {"CODE":"q01","NAME":"","TYPE_ID":2,"DISPLAY_ORDER":0, "_TF_ANSWERS":
                [
                  {ANSWER:"Never"},
                   {ANsWerer"Rarely"}
                 ]
             },
            {
              // Q3. How often do you feel that deadlines are unrealistic?
               "CODE":"q03","NAME":"","TYPE_ID:1,"DISPLAY_ORDER":2, "_TF_ANSWERS":
                [
                  {"ANSWER:"Never"},
                   {ANsWerer"Rarely"}
                 ]
             },
            {
              // Q5. How often do you feel that your work is not recognized or appreciated?
               "CODE":"q05","NAME":"","TYPE_ID:1,"DISPLAY_ORDER":4, "_TF_ANSWERS":
                [
                  {"ANSWER:"Never"},
                   {ANsWerer"Rarely"}
                 ]
             },
            {
              // Q7. How often do you feel that your work-life balance is compromised?
               "CODE":"q07","NAME":"","TYPE_ID:1,"DISPLAY_ORDER":6, "_TF_ANSWERS":
                [
                  {"ANSWER:"Never"},
                   {ANsWerer"Rarely"}
                 ]
             }
          ]

        }

      ]



```

This questionnaire has 4 questions that assess the frequency of feeling overwhelmed by workload (Q01), unrealistic deadlines(Q03) and lack recognition or appreciation for work, as well a compromise on Work-Life balance.

```json
{
  "data": {

      [
        {
          "CODE":"RR",
         NAME"Recognition and Rewards Questionnaire", 
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _T F_QUESTIONS":[...]
       }
     ]
   }

Questionaire Content:

1. The first question is about the importance of recognition.
2. Next, we have a series questions that ask for opinions on different types
    *  Of Recognition and Rewards (e.g., public acknowledgement vs private 
      feedback).
3. Then there are some open-ended text fields to gather more information from respondents.

Here's how it looks in JSON format:
```json

{
"data": {
"TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
[
{"CODE":"RR",
 "NAME":"",
  TYPE_ID:1,
   _T F_QUESTIONS":[

What do you think is the most important aspect of recognition and rewards? 
",TYPE ID :3,DISPLAY ORDER":0,"TF_ANSWERS":

{"ANSWER":"Public Acknowledgement"},

]
},
{
  {CODE: Q002,
   Name:"Do public recognitions have a positive impact on employees' morale?",
    TYPE_ID:1
     TF_QUESTIONS":[...]}
```

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

             'name':'What do you think is the biggest benefit of Smart working?',
              '_type_id' : 2, // Multiple Choice
               '__display_order__ ':0,

                '_'answers':
                  [
                    {'answer':"Increased productivity"},
                     { "Better work-life balance" },
                      {"More flexibility"}
                   ]
          },

         {
            'code': 'Q4',
             'name':'Do you feel that Smart working has improved your overall job satisfaction?',
              '_type_id' : 1, // Single Choice
               '__display_order__ ':0,

                '_'answers':
                  [
                    {'answer':"Yes"},
                     { "No" },
                      {"Don't know"}
                   ]
          },

         {
            'code': 'Q5',
             'name':'What do you think is the biggest challenge of Smart working?',
              '_type_id' : 2, // Multiple Choice
               '__display_order__ ':0,

                '_'answers':
                  [
                    {'answer':"Communication and collaboration"},
                     { "Technical issues" },
                      {"Blurred boundaries between work-life"}
                   ]
          }

       ]

    }]
}
```

This questionnaire includes five questions that cover various aspects of Smart working, such as the concept itself,
the frequency with which employees engage in remote or flexible
work arrangements,

their perception about its benefits and drawbacks.

Feel free to modify it according your needs.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Teambuilding initiatives feedback

-------------------

    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":

        {

          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
           _TF_QUESTIONS:
            [ 
              {  
                CODE: "",
               NAME:"",
                 TYPE_ID :1, // ID
                  DISPLAY_ORDER:'',
                    ANSWERS:[
                      {"ANSWER":""},
                     ]
             },
{
  QUESTION_NAME:"How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our teambuilding initiatives?",
   OPTIONS:["Very effective", "Somewhat Effective","Not very effectve"],
    REQUIRED: true,
     TYPE_ID :3, // Rating
      DISPLAY_ORDER:'',
       ANSWERS:[
         {"ANSWER":""},

},

     TYPE_ID :2, // Multiple Choice

Generate me a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I structured this JSON-formatted Questionnaire for you!

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"TRD001",
          "NAME":"'Training &amp;Development Program Evaluation'",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
          "_TF_QUESTIONS":[

            // Section: Training Objectives and Goals
            
              {"code":"Q1", 
               "name":"+ What are the primary objectives of your training programs?",  
                "type_id" : 2,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {answer:"To improve employee skills"},
                   { answer :" To enhance job performance"},    
                    ]
             },
            
            // Section: Training Methods and Materials
            
              {"code":"Q3", 
               name:"+ What methods do you currently use for training?",  
                "type_id" : 1,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {answer:"Classroom instruction"},
                   { answer :" On-the-job mentoring"},    
                    ]
             },
            
            // Section: Training Evaluation
            
              {"code":"Q5", 
               name:"+ How do you currently evaluate the effectiveness of your training programs?",  
                "type_id" : 2,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {answer:"Surveys and feedback forms"},
                   { answer :" Performance reviews"},    
                    ]
             },
            
            // Section: Training Frequency
            
              {"code":"Q7", 
               name:"+ How often do you provide training to your employees?",  
                "type_id" : 1,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {answer:"Daily or weekly"},
                   { answer :" Monthly"} ,    
                    ]
             },
            
            // Section: Training Budget
            
              {"code":"Q9", 
               name:"+ What is the average budget for training programs in your organization?",  
                "type_id" : 8,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {
                     ANSWER:"Less than $1K"
                   },    
                    ]
             },
            
            // Section: Training Challenges
            
              {"code":"Q11", 
               name:"+ What are the biggest challenges you face when implementing training programs?",  
                "type_id" : 4,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {answer="Lack of employee participation"},
                   {
                     ANSWER:"Difficulty in measuring ROI"
                    },    
                      ]
             },
            
            // Section: Training Future Plans
            
              {"code":"Q13", 
               name:"+ What are your plans for future training and development programs?",  
                "type_id" : 1,   
                 _tf_answers:[
                  {answer="Increase frequency of trainings"},
                   {
                     ANSWER:"Expand to new departments"
                    },    
                      ]
             }
          ] // end TF_QUESTIONS
        } 
      ]

    }

}
```

This questionnaire is designed for evaluating the effectiveness and planning future training programs. It covers various aspects such as objectives, methods used in current trainings (classroom instruction or on-the-job mentoring), evaluation of their performance reviews) , frequency provided to employees daily/weekly/monthly).

{
  'data': {
    '_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES':
      [
        { 
          'CODE':'WLBBALANCE',
          'NAME':"How do I achieve WorkLife Balance?",
          'TYPE_ID' :3,
        	'_tf_questions__':
        	       [  
            {'code': "Q1",  // Question Code
              '_name_':   "I am satisfied with my current work-life balance.", 
               TYPE_:      {id:2, description:"Scale (5-point)"} ,// Scale question type.
                'display_order' :0,
                 "_tf_answers_" :
                  [
                    {'answer':"Strongly Disagree"},
                     {"Answer":1},
                      "Somewhat Agree",
                       3,"Neutral"
                        Somewhere disagree

                           {
                             Answer:4, 
                            }
                              } ,// End of Quesiton

            // Add more questions here...
          ]
        }]
      }

```

Here's how the questionnaire is structured:

1. The root object contains a single property 'data'.
   - This data has two properties.
     2nd one named '_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' which holds an array of objects, each representing
       A WorkLife Balance Questionnaire.

3rd Property: CODE (string) for the questionnaire's unique code and NAME(string)
    to represent its name. TYPE_ID(int), set equal to 'Work-Life-Balance', 
   - '_tf_questions_' is a JSON object that contains an array of objects, each representing
     A question in this WorkLife Balance Questionnaire.

4th Property: Each answer has the following properties:
  * CODE(string) for its unique code.
    NAME (string), which represents content. TYPE_ID(int)
   - '_tf_answers_' is a JSON object that contains an array of objects, each representing
     A possible response to this WorkLife Balance Questionnaire.

5th Property: Each answer has the following properties:
  * CODE(string) for its unique code.
    NAME (string), which represents content. TYPE_ID(int)
   - '_tf_answers_' is a JSON object that contains an array of objects, each representing
     A possible response to this WorkLife Balance Questionnaire.

            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100055
     - Topic: Workload Management
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workload Management

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I structured this JSON-based Questionnaire for you:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WL001",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _tf_questions:[
              {"code":"","name","How would rate your current workload?"},
               ["_answers":[{"answer"="1 - Too High"},{"{"2- Manageable"}},{"{0.5}"]}],
             {
                code:"",
                 name:"Do you feel overwhelmed by the amount of work assigned to you?",
                  type:4,
                   _tf_answers:[ {"answe":"Strongly Agree"}, { "Agree", },  ]
              },
            ...
```
The questionnaire is structured as follows:

1. The root object contains a single property 'data'.
2. Within this data, there's an array of questionnaires with the key '_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'. In our case we have only one.
3. This main Questionnaire has properties: CODE (unique code), NAME(name given to questionnaire) and TYPE_ID which is equal 1 for Workload Management.

4.'_tf_questions' represents a list where each item in this array corresponds with an individual question within the survey, including its unique identifier 'code', content ('name'), type ID(6-8 representing different types of questions), display order('display_order') and possible answers('_TF_ANSWERS').

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based Questionnaire for you, as per our agreed-upon format.

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WORKPLACE_CULTURE",
          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
          

```

Here's the actual questionnaire content:

**Workplace Culture Questionnaire**

This survey aims to understand your perceptions and experiences of our workplace culture. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement, recognize strengths, and create a more positive work environment.

```json
{
  "_TF_QUESTIONS":
    [
      {
        "CODE":"Q1",
        "NAME":"How would you rate the overall morale in your team?",
        
```

Here are some questions to get started:

**Morale**

* ID: How do I feel about my job? (Scale from Very Satisfied - Neutral)
	+ Answer Options:
      {
       "_TF_ANSWERS":
        [
          {"ANSWER":"Very satisfied"},
          {{"Slightly dissatisfie"},{"Neutral"}},
          {"Dissatisified"}
```

**Communication**

* ID: How often do you feel informed about important company decisions?
    + One answer from the list below
      {
       "_TF_ANSWERS":
        [
         "Always",
           ["Mostly",],
            {{"Sometimes","Rarely"}}
```

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
