     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based questionnaire for you:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WKC001",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _TF_QUESTIONS":[...]
         }
       ]
     }

```

Here is the generated JSON questionnaire on Workplace Culture:

```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WKC001",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _TF_QUESTIONS":[

              // Question1 - Multiple Choice (Type ID = 2)
               {" CODE ":"WKC101", 
                " NAME ":"
What does 'Workplace Culture' mean to you? ",  
                 "_ TF_ANSWERS": [
                  {ANSWER:"A positive and supportive environment"},   
                   { ANSWER: A place where everyone is treated equally},    
                    { ANSWE R : An atmosphere that encourages collaboration"} 
                ]
               },


              // Question2 - Rating (Type ID = 3)
                 {" CODE ":"WKC102",  
                  " NAME ":"
How would you rate your overall job satisfaction?",   
                   "_ TF_ANSWERS": [
                     {
                       ANSWER:1,NAME:"Very Satisfied" 
                    },
                      {ANSWER :5,"Name":"Not at all satisfied"}
                ]
               },


              // Question3 - Open-Ended (Type ID = 4)
                 {" CODE ":"WKC103",  
                  " NAME ":"
What do you think is the most important aspect of our workplace culture?",   
                   "_ TF_ANSWERS": [
                     {
                       ANSWER:"Please provide your answer in this text box."
                    }
                ]
               },


              // Question3 - Ranking (Type ID = 6)
                 {" CODE ":"WKC104",  
                  " NAME ":"
Rank the following aspects of our workplace culture from most important to least:",   
                   "_ TF_ANSWERS": [
                     {
                       ANSWER:1,NAME:"Collaboration" 
                    },
                      {ANSWER :2,"Name":"Communication"},
                        {" ANSWE R ":"3"," Name " :"Recognition"}
                ]
               }
            ]

         }

       ]



```

This questionnaire is designed to assess the workplace culture of your organization. It includes a mix of multiple-choice, rating scale and open-ended questions that will help you gauge employee perceptions about their work environment.

The first question asks employees what they think 'Workplace Culture' means to them.
Then it rates job satisfaction on an 1-5 point Likert Scale (Type ID =3).
Next is the Open Ended Question where respondents can provide a written answer, and finally there's Ranking type of questions that will help you understand which aspects are most important.

Please note: The actual question content may vary based upon your specific needs.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.

Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I structured this JSON-formatted Questionnaire for you:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WORKPLACE_CULTURE",
          "NAME":"",
           TYPE_ID:3,
            _TF_QUESTIONS":[

              // Section - Introduction to Workplace Culture 
             {  
               CODE:"INTRO_WC",   
                NAME:"",
                 DISPLAY_ORDER :1,    
                  "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      {"ANSWER":"I'm excited about the company culture"},
                       {"ANSWER","Not really"}
                     ]
                   },
              // Section - Communication
            {
           "CODE": "",
             "NAME":"",
               TYPE_ID:2,
                _DISPLAY_ORDER : 3,    
                 "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      { 
                        ANSWER:"I feel comfortable sharing my ideas with colleagues"},
                       {"ANSWER","Sometimes I do but not always"}
                     ]
                   },
              // Section - Collaboration
            {
           "CODE": "",
             NAME:"",
               TYPE_ID:1,
                _DISPLAY_ORDER : 5,    
                 "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      { 
                        ANSWER:"I feel supported by my team"},
                       {"ANSWER","Not really"}
                     ]
                   },
              // Section - Feedback
            {
           "CODE": "",
             NAME:"",
               TYPE_ID:4,
                _DISPLAY_ORDER : 7,    
                 "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      { 
                        ANSWER:"I feel like my feedback is valued"},
                       {"ANSWER","Not really"}
                     ]
                   },
              // Section - Recognition
            {
           "CODE": "",
             NAME:"",
               TYPE_ID:1,
                _DISPLAY_ORDER : 9,    
                 "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      { 
                        ANSWER:"I feel recognized for my contributions"},
                       {"ANSWER","Not really"}
                     ]
                   },
              // Section - Growth
            {
           "CODE": "",
             NAME:"",
               TYPE_ID:2,
                _DISPLAY_ORDER : 11,    
                 "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      { 
                        ANSWER:"I feel like I have opportunities for growth"},
                       {"ANSWER","Not really"}
                     ]
                   },
              // Section - Conclusion
            {
           "CODE": "",
             NAME:"",
               TYPE_ID:1,
                _DISPLAY_ORDER : 13,    
                 "_TF_ANSWERS":
                    [
                      { 
                        ANSWER:"I'm satisfied with the company culture"},
                       {"ANSWER","Not really"}
                     ]
                   }
              ]

          }

      ]



}
```
This questionnaire is designed to gauge your perception of workplace culture.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation:

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based Questionnaire for you:
```
{
  "data": {
    "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
      [
        {
          "CODE":"WPCULTURE",
          "NAME":"",
          "TYPE_ID":3,
           _tf_questions:[
             {"code":"","name","How would rate the overall work environment in your department?",type:1,display_order,"",answers:[{"answer"}]},
            ]
         }
       ]

}
```

Here's a sample questionnaire on Workplace Culture:

```json
{
  "data":
    {
      "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
        {

          // Questionnaire Code and Name

           CODE:"WPCULTURE",
           NAME: "Workplace Culture Survey",

          TYPE_ID :3,

            _tf_questions:[
              {"code":"Q1","name":"","How would you rate the overall work environment in your department?"},
               {
                 code:"",
                name,"What do think is most important for a positive workplace culture?",
                  type,
                   2,answers:[]},
             ]
           }
         ]

}
```

Here's how I've structured this JSON-based Questionnaire:

1. The root of the questionnaire object contains only one property 'data'.
   - This data has two properties:
     * '_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array that holds a single element, which represents our Workplace Culture Survey.
       It includes information about code and name for your survey.

2. Each question in this JSON-based Questionnaire follows the same structure:

    1- The 'CODE': (string) - This property contains each individual's unique ID or any other identifier you may want to use within a questionnaire, such as "Q3" etc.
      *   It is used for identifying specific questions.

2. Each question also includes these properties:
     • '_NAME' : string: The content of the survey (e.g., 'How would rate your overall job satisfaction?').
       - This property represents each individual's unique ID or any other identifier you may want to use within a questionnaire, such as "Q3" etc.
         It is used for identifying specific questions.

     • '_TYPE_ID' : int: The type of question (e.g., 1-8).
        *   Each possible answer in this JSON-based Questionnaire has the following properties:
          - 'CODE': string
            This property contains each individual's unique ID or any other identifier you may want to use within a questionnaire, such as "Q3" etc.
              It is used for identifying specific questions.

     • '_DISPLAY_ORDER' : int: The display order of your question (e.g., 1-10).
        *   Each possible answer in this JSON-based Questionnaire has the following properties:
          - 'CODE': string
            This property contains each individual's unique ID or any other identifier you may want to use within a questionnaire, such as "Q3" etc.
              It is used for identifying specific questions.

     • '_TF_ANSWERS' : array: An object representing possible answers (e.g., 1-5).
        *   Each answer in this JSON-based Questionnaire has the following properties:
          - 'ANSWER': string
            This property contains each individual's unique ID or any other identifier you may want to use within a questionnaire, such as "Q3" etc.
              It is used for identifying specific questions.

I hope that helps!

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment
